Gold Shop Owner Lin Bingyan Kidnapped 117

Returning Home After Dinner at Jue Lu

Suddenly Kidnapped by Bandits After Getting Into the Car

Lin Bingyan, a Guangdong native, runs the gold business. Hengxing at 36 Edward Road and Jia Shengda at 2 Jiujiang Road are both operated by Lin, which makes him a target for kidnappers. At about 8:15 last night, Lin was kidnapped by bandits at the intersection of Kunshan Road, and his whereabouts are unknown. Lin lives at 13 Arui Lane, North Sichuan Road, in the Chinese area. He has a car, and the license number is Municipal Government 2010 and Concession 10086. The driver, named Wensheng, has been driving for many years. Lin goes out early and returns late every day, and Lin uses this car as transportation. After finishing his business in the afternoon, Lin goes to Jue Lu at 277 Kunshan Road, North Sichuan Road, for entertainment, which is his usual practice. Yesterday evening, Lin rested at Jue Lu as usual and had dinner. At about 8:10, Lin wanted to return and ordered Wensheng to wait with the car. When Lin got into the car, four bandits suddenly appeared, each holding a pistol, watching the driver and his assistant, prohibiting them from shouting, and driving them out of the car. They dragged the victim into the car and drove west, turning south from North Sichuan Road and driving away. In an instant, they disappeared. The driver's assistant reported to the Hongkou Police Station, and the police immediately dispatched detectives to search for the victim. Lin Bingyan, the victim, is 41 years old. Before coming to Shanghai, he ran a gold business in Hong Kong. Many people in the gold industry in Shanghai know him well.

Heavy Fog in Shanghai Yesterday 118

China Merchants Bureau Ships Suspended

Airlines Also Suspended

There was heavy fog in Shanghai yesterday, which did not dissipate from morning to noon and did not recede until dusk. The Huangpu and Suzhou Rivers were shrouded in dense fog, and ships could not be seen beyond fifty steps. The road was white and boundless, and pedestrians on the road also felt very difficult because vehicles were not easy to identify. The ships of the China Merchants Bureau that were scheduled to depart yesterday, including Yushun to Haizhou, Xinfeng to Weihaiwei and then to Yantai and Tianjin, Haiyan to Wenzhou, Jiangda along the Yangtze River, and Xinjiangtian to Ningbo, were all suspended due to fog and will depart another day. Jiangda, which was scheduled to arrive in Shanghai yesterday, also did not arrive due to fog. Changxing's Canada had not yet left the port by 6:00 PM. In addition, more than 30 ships, including the Russian Empress, Jardine Matheson's Fulsheng, and Taikoo's Zhejiang, which could have entered the port in Japan yesterday, were anchored at the Wusongkou anchorage, waiting to enter the port after the fog dissipated today. The China National Aviation Corporation's planes from Shanghai to Beijing and from Beijing to Shanghai were also suspended due to fog yesterday.

Patrolmen Involved in Kidnapping 119

Helping to Transport Guns

Tried in the Kidnapping Case

Jin Yangjin, a Chinese detective of the Jing'an Temple Police Station, and others previously arrested a large number of male and female bandits, including Shan Yaonan, at 50 Taopeng Lane, Taopeng Road, and sent them to the First Special District Court for trial. It has been recorded in this newspaper that the Western and Chinese detectives in charge of this case interrogated the arrested criminals. According to the confession of the ninth defendant, Gu Chenshi, the eighth defendant, Wang Hailan, had used a gun to rob a certain family surnamed at 897 Maigen Road on the 28th of last month. After the incident, she was given a gold watch and five yuan in paper money. However, when the robbery occurred, two guns were transported by Gao Xinpu, a native of Anhui who was serving as a Chinese policeman with number 1986. The Western and Chinese detectives investigated and found that the Chinese policeman was currently serving at the Huizi Police Station, so they telegraphed the head of the Huizi Police Station to detain Officer Gao. They also took the defendants Gu Chenshi and Wang Hailan to the police station to identify Officer Gao among the other ten policemen. Gu and Wang pointed out Officer Gao, so he was taken back to the police station and detained. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Second Criminal Court of the Special Court. The police station's lawyer, Wang Yaotang, stated the case, saying that after the defendant Gao Xinpu was arrested, Gao denied helping to transport firearms at the police station. He said that between March and April of this year, he was serving at the General Police Station. One day on the way to inspect pedestrians, he saw that Gu Chenshi and Wang Hailan looked suspicious, so he searched them. Wang was unwilling and was slapped several times, resulting in a grudge. Now, she is falsely accusing him. The defendants Gu Chenshi and Wang Hailan successively surrendered to the court and confessed that before the robbery on Maigen Road, they first discussed the matter in the four-story building behind the Great World in the French Concession. Ren Jinbiao, the seventh defendant, handed over a gun to Gu Chenshi to transport to the four-story building and transfer it to the defendant Gao Xinpu. Gao and a stout man with a hemp coat went out at about 4:00 and did not return until 8:00, still handing the gun to Gu Chenshi to take back. However, she was timid and afraid that something would happen on the way, so she refused to carry it, so the defendant took it to Wang Hailan's house. The defendant denied what they said. Judge Feng Shide verified the confession and ordered Officer Gao to be detained for a retrial on the 17th of this month with Shan Yaonan and others.

Rumors That the Lost Son of a Widow Is Still Alive 120

Did Not Drown in the River

Zhu Songlin Confessed the Truth

Yao Zhusheng Was Indeed Framed

Ju Sheng, the eight-year-old son of the widow Yao Gu, was kidnapped by bandits at the entrance of his grandmother's house at 96 An'nan Road on July 7 of this year and a ransom was demanded. Jin Yangwu, a Chinese detective from the Jing'an Temple Police Station, and others arrested two suspects in the case, Zhu Songlin and Lu Wangshi, and sent them to the Special Court. Zhu confessed that he had kidnapped Yao Jusheng, but that Jusheng had drowned in the Huangpu River. He also said that the mastermind of the case was Yao Zhusheng, the clan chief of Yao, and that Lu Wangshi had no connection with the case. The court ordered Zhu to be detained and released on bail. Later, the police arrested Yao Zhusheng and interrogated him several times, but it was still inconclusive. During the last court trial, Zhu Songlin suddenly changed his testimony, saying that the child Yao Jusheng had not drowned and had been fostered on a boat of a boatman surnamed in Huangpu River in Pudong. The Western and Chinese detectives went to search for him at the address for a long time, but there was still no trace. Therefore, the life and death of Yao Jusheng is still in doubt. At 2:30 yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Tingqi came to the Second Criminal Court again for a retrial. The family of the victim hired lawyer Chen Tingrui, and the court appointed Ye Fikang as Zhu Songlin's pro bono lawyer. Yao Zhusheng hired two lawyers, Tao Wuzhi and Yu Hualong, to defend him in court. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, stated that since the defendant Zhu Songlin confessed the whereabouts of the child last time, the police immediately ordered detectives to search, but the result was nothing, which shows that Zhu's confession is unreliable. Judge Wu then interrogated Zhu. According to Zhu, the child Yao Jusheng did die. After he kidnapped Jusheng, he secretly fostered him on the boat of Lu Bingsheng, Xiaohua, and a person surnamed Yu. The boat was parked near the Hufeng Warehouse in Pudong. Fearing that it would be exposed, he dressed Jusheng in women's clothing and put a gold ring on his left ear. He took off the pair of slippers that Jusheng was wearing and prepared to send them to his grandmother. On the way, he turned to his home in Liuliqiao, Pudong. His wife saw him and asked him about it. He told her the truth. His wife made a lot of noise, so he falsely claimed that the child had drowned in the Huangpu River. Yao Zhusheng and Lu Wangshi were all falsely accused and had nothing to do with the case. His formal accomplices were Lu, Dong, Yu, and others. What he said today is all true and there are no falsehoods. Yao Zhusheng confessed that he was indeed framed by Zhu, but he has suffered a lot. After the interrogation, all the witnesses have been examined. The lawyers from all parties then stood up and debated for a long time. At the end, Prosecutor Li Ying expressed his opinion. Judge Wu announced that the debate in this case was over and that the verdict would be announced at 2:00 PM on the 15th of this month. Yao Zhusheng was released on bail pending further summons.

Report on the Disaster Relief Efforts of the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association in Jiangbei 121

This time, the provinces suffered from unprecedented floods. In the Jiangbei area, there are still areas where the water has not receded. The Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Relief Association is making every effort to carry out emergency winter relief. In addition to the joint associations in Hankou and other ports, as well as branches specially set up in Wuhu and the severely affected areas in northern Anhui, it also attaches great importance to the Jiangbei area. Branches have been successively established in Yangzhou, Gaoyou, Taixian, Dongtai, Xinghua, Yancheng, Huaiyin, and Huai'an to actively provide relief. Cotton clothes are also being distributed in Baoying, Jiangpu, and other counties. Recently, many reports have been received from various branches. The report from the Yancheng branch is transcribed below. "Respectfully, this year's flood has exceeded the flood of the 10th year of the Republic of China. The number of houses that have been washed away is particularly large. We are entrusted by your association to handle the Yancheng relief work, and we should do our best to investigate and distribute the supplies properly. The details of the first distribution and the recent distribution situation, as well as the urgent need for relief among the disaster victims, are briefly described below. The first relief fund of 12,000 yuan, in addition to 2,000 yuan for emergency relief and medicines, the remaining 10,000 yuan and winter clothes were distributed in five districts. Because there are many disaster victims and the disaster area is very wide, the relief fund is limited. If it is distributed to everyone, each person will receive very little, which is not very helpful. Therefore, we first chose to distribute it in the first, second, seventh, eleventh, and thirteenth districts (Yancheng has a total of fourteen districts). Now we have received a second relief fund of 20,000 yuan and winter clothes, and we have been instructed to contact the National Government Relief Committee to discuss the distribution plan. We have already contacted them and decided to adopt the universal distribution method. We will use the rotating universal distribution method. Therefore, this time, we will investigate and distribute it in the third, ninth, twelfth, and fourteenth districts. Next time, we will investigate and distribute it in the fourth, fifth, sixth, eighth, and tenth districts, so that the entire county will be covered. It is not that we do not want to distribute it to everyone each time, but it is like using a cup of water to put out a fire, which will only arouse public resentment. Therefore, we have adopted the rotating distribution method so that the disaster victims can survive for a few days or a dozen days after receiving the relief. Most of the disaster victims distributed this time are extremely poor families. The cold winter is coming soon, and the poor will soon run out of food. The famine situation next spring is expected to be a hundred times worse than this year. The requests for relief have already piled up like snowflakes. We hope that more relief funds will be added to meet the needs of relief. In addition, 10,000 gold coins should be provided to provide more assistance, as the effect is very good. The poor and sick are becoming more and more numerous. The health team is only set up in the city, while the countryside is suffering from lack of relief. "

New Building of Renji Hospital to be Completed 122

Patients Can Move in Before Christmas

Completion Ceremony to Be Held in January

According to the "North China Daily News," the new building of Renji Hospital on Shandong Road is now largely completed. It is expected that patients will be moved in before Christmas. The official completion ceremony will be held in January next year. The new building can currently accommodate 200 patients. With an increase in nurses in the future, it is expected to accommodate up to 270 patients. The top floor of the new hospital is the kitchen, the sixth floor is for staff dormitories, most of the fifth floor is used for medical research, the fourth floor has four operating rooms, and the obstetrics and gynecology ward is also located there. The third floor is for wards and delivery rooms, the second floor is for X-ray and operating rooms, dispensaries, special beds, and clinics for dentistry, ENT, and dermatology, as well as a women's clinic. The men's clinic and emergency room are on the first floor.

Representatives of Fili Lace Industry Petition in Beijing for Exemption from Business Tax 126

According to Guomin She, Fili lace, produced in Pudong, Wuxi, Rugao, and other places, is a kind of Chinese-made product woven from cotton thread into a net-like pattern. It is mainly exported to Europe and the United States, with an annual export value of about one million. Most of the businesses are located in the Pudong area, hence the organization of the Chuansha Fili Lace Industry Association. Recently, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance intends to levy a 5/1000 business tax on the industry. The industry believes that this lace is a handicraft made by rural women, and imposing a heavy tax would directly affect the national economy and the people's livelihood and indirectly hinder foreign trade. They believe that Fili lace qualifies as a tax-exempt item. Based on various reasons, they have sent representatives to Beijing overnight with official documents to petition the Ministries of Industry and Finance. At the same time, they are also preparing to request the Ministry of Industry to rectify the production of Fili lace and provide protection, with the aim of actively developing exports.

Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities Reissues Vehicle Licenses 127

Bicycles... Starting from December 16th

Other Vehicles... Starting from December 25th

For the convenience of inspection, the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities issues a vehicle license for each type of vehicle. As the validity period of the licenses issued this year is about to expire, new licenses for the 21st year will be reissued, except for small carts. Bicycles will be reissued starting from December 16th, and all other types of vehicles will be reissued starting from December 25th. The procedures are as follows: (1) Each vehicle owner should, before paying the first installment of the 21st year donation, take the old license to the original vehicle office to exchange for a new license. (2) A license fee should be paid during the exchange. The fees are: silver 3 jiao per license for automobiles, motorized bicycles, private rickshaws, and horse-drawn carriages; silver 2 jiao per license for manure carts and freight trucks. Motorized bicycles will also return the old license plate and receive a new license plate at the same time. Subsequent license plate changes will be made once a year without additional fees. (3) The license plate and license for bicycles cost a total of silver 5 jiao. This has been announced.

Zhang Zhidong Advocates Life Insurance 128

Zhang Zhijiang, the Pacification Commissioner of Jiangsu and Director of the Chinese National Martial Arts Hall, hosted a banquet at the Zhongshe on Weihaiwei Road the other day, inviting celebrities from Shanghai and business leaders to promote Chinese life insurance. More than 20 people attended, including Shi Liangcai, Song Zijing, Qu Wenliu, Lan Ting, Xu Xinliu, Huang Hanzhi, Yuan Ludeng, Wu Yunzhai, Ji Yunqing, Wang Binyan, Xiang Songmao, Wu Zhihao, Ren Huageng, Shen Sizhuang, and Yang Wuxin. During the banquet, Zhang first raised his glass to wish everyone good health and talked about life insurance as a new undertaking with both public welfare and commercial aspects in China today. At a time when everyone is advocating domestic products, the Ningshao Life Insurance Company, with its substantial capital, capable personnel, and precise organization, has emerged to recover rights and interests, protect individual production, promote local stability, and strive to strengthen physical health. This kind of undertaking is very much in line with my aspirations to promote national martial arts and the responsibility of maintaining peace and quiet in the locality. Therefore, I am willing to do my best to promote its success and hope that people from all walks of life will jointly promote it to achieve popularity. Then, Hu Yongqi, the general manager of Ningshao Life Insurance Company, stood up and talked about the history of the life insurance business. He briefly stated that life insurance originated in the United Kingdom and gradually spread to Europe and the United States after it was initially a mutual aid system. Nowadays, Germany has gone further and is operated by the government, called social insurance, to assist the rule of law in the country. Recently, the development of the life insurance business in the United States is the best in the world, providing considerable protection for the three major problems that everyone cannot avoid: "illness," "old age," and "death." Therefore, the country is rich and strong, society is peaceful, and life is happy. Ningshao Company adopts the most scientific methods of American insurance companies, and the investment is even more cautious. As for the income and expenditure accounts, they are completely open to show good faith. Now, let me briefly state the three differences between Chinese insurance companies and foreign insurance companies as follows: (1) Chinese companies have lower premiums; (2) Chinese company policies are in Chinese, which is easy to understand; (3) Chinese companies are subject to Chinese law. Therefore, I hope that leaders from all walks of life will promote and advocate it. Then, Yuan Ludeng talked about the past failures of the Chinese insurance business. The reason is that the people who run it do not understand the principles of insurance and use scientific methods, which makes the general public suspicious and dare not try it. Now, Ningshao Company, with a long time of preparation and a very precise organization, comes out to serve the society and will surely live up to the public's elegant intention of loving national assets and businesses. Then, Shen Sizhuang gave a speech, briefly stating that those of us who advocate life insurance are serious and strict in handling affairs. The general public thinks that Chinese companies can all be perfunctory, but Ningshao Company is not. For several weeks, judging from the strict physical examination alone, it is enough to show the precision of its system. Secondly, from an economic point of view, (1) prudent investment (2) open accounts, judging from the above points, I, as a third party and the insured, am willing to introduce and promote it with 12 points of faith. I hope that leaders from all walks of life will jointly introduce, promote, and insure, and then the development of Chinese businesses can be predicted. It dispersed at ten o'clock.

Huacheng Tobacco Company Offers a Reward of 10,000 Yuan 129

Stopped Trading with Japanese Merchants Long Ago After the Wanbaoshan Incident

Willing to Pay a Fine of 10,000 Yuan If Undeniable Evidence is Provided

The raw materials and printed materials used in the various cigarettes produced by Huacheng Tobacco Company are not enemy goods. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, the National Goods League, the Cigarette Factory Association, the Color Printing Industry Association, and other groups have investigated and confirmed that they are indeed genuine domestic goods. Recently, in a case where a zinc plate was stolen from a Japanese rubber printing shop, it was found that there was a zinc plate for printing the company's Beauty brand cigarettes. Unscrupulous people have taken the opportunity to wantonly slander and even sent letters to the company to question it. Now, in order to express its sincerity, the company has offered a reward of 10,000 yuan. Anyone who can provide evidence to prove that Huacheng still trades with Japanese merchants after the boycott, after being verified by a legitimate merchant group, is willing to pay a fine of 10,000 yuan. If there are rumors and deliberate slanders, the company will ask the fellow law firm to file a lawsuit and severely punish the rumor-mongers.

Qingliange Shop Owner and Concubine Involved in Lawsuit Retrial 131

Both Sides Invite Witnesses

Sun Yunqing Is Ashamed of Being Old

Sun Yunqing, the owner of the Qingliange shopping mall, is over sixty years old. His third concubine, Jiang Cuiling, is beautiful and young, which is quite pitiful. On July 24th of this year, Jiang suddenly left. She then hired lawyer Chen Bingxing to negotiate with Sun, proposing conditions for separation. Sun did not accept because her demands were too harsh. Jiang then filed a criminal complaint against Sun for abuse and battery. At the end of the first trial, the plaintiff's claim was dismissed. Jiang was not satisfied and filed an appeal. As a result of the second trial, Sun Yunqing was fined 50 yuan. Sun was also not satisfied and filed a third trial appeal to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The result was that the case was returned to the court of the second trial for a retrial. Yesterday afternoon, Zhou Han, the chief of the criminal court of the First Special District Court, and two judges, Feng and Shen, specially convened a collegiate panel for the retrial. Sun's lawyers, Ni Zheng'ou and Zhang Deqin, and Jiang's lawyer, Chen Bingxing, all appeared in court, and both parties and their witnesses were also present. First, Jiang Cuiling recounted the incident of being beaten by Sun on July 22nd. Then, her close friend, Zhu Lindi, testified that she was also present and witnessed Sun beating Jiang on the day in question. Then, Dr. Chen testified that he treated Jiang several times and diagnosed that she was injured in the buttocks. Then, Sun's witness, Zhu Wu (i.e., Lindi's mother), claimed that Sun and Jiang had always been harmonious and Sun had never abused her. Her daughter, Lindi, did not go to Sun's house on July 22nd, and all her statements were false. Xu Shiping testified that he was a friend of Sun and that Sun had asked him to persuade Jiang to return. He witnessed Sun and Jiang talking, and Jiang did not say that Sun beat her on that day, only saying why they fought last year, but Sun denied it all. Jiang did not say anything else. Finally, Sun Yunqing gave a detailed account of the beginning and end of the incident. He seemed quite angry when he spoke, saying that it was all because he was old and worthless. He still sobbed after the statement. After the lawyers of both sides debated each other, the judge ordered that the sentence be announced on the 14th.

Gao Qiaosong Hires a Maidservant and Attempts Rape 133

Gao Qiaosong from Fengjing used to work as a partner at Deshunxiang Foreign Goods Store on Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession, but was dismissed due to his absurdity. Gao is over thirty years old and still a widower. Recently, he had a whimsical idea and rented a stone-gate building at No. 51 Qinyefang on Route Ghisi in West Shanghai. All the furniture was rented from a rental shop, deliberately creating a lavish scene. Those who did not know thought it was a wealthy family. When he moved in, relatives such as wet nurses and aunts came to help with the arrangements. A few days ago, Gao entrusted Lao Deji Matchmaker Shop in Avenue Edward VII, whom he knew well, to hire a maidservant, who must be young and beautiful. He chose Xu Sanmei, who was 22 years old (Xu was from the North Gate of Qingpu and had been promised to a Sun family). The matchmaker agreed on a monthly salary of six yuan. Unexpectedly, after Sanmei entered the door to work, she saw that the female guests had dispersed in the evening, leaving only the master and servant. After dinner, Gao said to Sanmei, "Have you married?" She replied, "Not yet." Gao said again, "I am not yet married either. Why don't you be my companion? It's better than a villager. Please don't refuse." Sanmei blushed when she heard this and did not say a word. Unexpectedly, Gao's animalistic nature surged and he could not stop himself. He actually tried to force her. Sanmei was quick-witted and made an excuse that she was having her period and that she would let him do as he pleased after it was over. Gao believed it to be true and reluctantly let go. Sanmei broke free and hired a car to go to her brother Yuan Kui's Yongxiang South Goods Store on Zhoujiazui to complain. Her brother, after hearing the news, rushed to report to the police and asked them to investigate.

Bank Teaboy Steals More Than 3,000 Yuan 136

Song Yexi, a native of Anhui, 18 years old this year, works as a teaboy at the China Industrial Bank at No. 563 Avenue Dubail. On October 9th, taking advantage of the cashier of the cashier's office being on leave and Kong Bingjun being assigned to replace him, he secretly made a key, opened the writing desk drawer, stole the key to the silver box, opened the box, and stole 3,800 yuan in cash to spend. The next day, Kong found out and reported it to the police for investigation, but the case was not solved. On the 24th of this month, Song deposited 230 yuan in the Jincheng Bank in the name of Shaolinji. All the remaining money was lost in gambling with friends. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the 22nd of last month, he stole a check for 105 yuan from the bank's manager, Sun Yangnong, and took it to the head office on Beijing Road to collect the money. The clerk noticed that the amount on the check was written as 105 yuan, but after checking the handwriting, it was different from Sun's. He then telegraphed Sun Yangnong, who replied that he had not issued the check and asked him to stop the payment and return the check. However, they did not yet know that Song had done it. Song took back the check and fled home in a guilty conscience. The bank then reported the incident to the police and asked them to investigate. Detective Mao Jinsheng and Detective Bao Jiang Changwen found out that both cases were committed by Song in collusion with his colleague Jian Shunrong. They knew that Song was hiding in his home at No. 18 Diandang Lane, Wansheng Bridge, Ximen, Huajie, and immediately dispatched detectives from the Public Security Bureau to go there together. Song and Jian were arrested, as well as Song's father, Song Hailin, and the secretly made keys and the Jincheng Bank passbook were seized. It was found that only 80 yuan was left, and the rest had been withdrawn. However, the check had been torn up and could not be retrieved. They were taken back to the police station. Yesterday afternoon, they were escorted to the Second Special Court. The police lawyer Gu Shouxi stated the facts of the case. The plaintiff, Kong Bingjun, and Sun Yangnong (represented by his younger brother Yao Dong), recounted the circumstances of the theft. When interrogated, Song Yexi confessed to the theft. Jian and Song's father denied collusion. Judge Xiong pushed for a postponement of the continued trial. The two defendants, Song and Jian, were detained. Song Hailin was released on bail to be available at any time. With no bail, he was detained.

Two Committee Members Resign from Anti-Japanese Association 142

Fang Jiaobo: Fang Jiaobo, a standing committee member of the Anti-Japanese Association, sent a letter to the association yesterday, saying: "To the esteemed association, this association is formed by people from all walks of life in the city and holds an important position. Since taking office as a standing committee member, I have been diligent day and night, never daring to slack off. Recently, the association's affairs have intensified, and the work has become frequent. Internally and externally, only competent individuals can shoulder this heavy responsibility. I consider myself mediocre and foolish, and it is impossible to be up to the task. If I were to carry out my duties perfunctorily, I would not be able to face the public. If I were to strive to make progress, I would feel that my talent and wisdom are insufficient. If I were to merely hold a false title, it would only delay the association's affairs and betray the trust placed in me. After repeated deliberation, I have no choice but to resign from my position as an executive committee member and all concurrent positions, so that the association can select talented individuals to actively advance the cause. Jiaobo will still, in my individual capacity, follow behind you all and participate in the patriotic movement. If it is within my ability, I will never shirk my responsibility. I hope that this resignation can be brought up in a meeting and approved. I am deeply grateful. This is addressed to the Executive Committee of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association."

Feng Shaoquan: Mr. Feng Shaoquan, an executive committee member and deputy director of the custody department of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of all circles in this city, has been diligently fulfilling his duties since taking office. Recently, due to his weak health, he is unable to cope with the heavy workload. Yesterday, he sent a letter to the Standing Committee of the Association, requesting to resign from his concurrent position in the custody department. The original letter is reproduced below: "To the esteemed association, I, Shaoquan, with my meager talents, was elected as an executive committee member of this association, and I already felt that I was not up to the task. Then, the esteemed association showed me even greater favor by additionally promoting me to serve as the deputy director of the custody department. I felt even more ashamed. However, at this time of national crisis, anti-Japanese work is a duty that every citizen should fulfill. Therefore, I also knew that I was not talented enough, but I rashly took on the responsibility. However, in the past few months, although I have exhausted my mind and wisdom, I have not achieved any results. I have truly failed to live up to the trust placed in me by the esteemed association, and I feel deeply ashamed. Recently, my health has deteriorated, and I am even less able to cope with the heavy workload. Therefore, I am specifically stating the reasons and sincerely requesting that you select other talented individuals and approve my resignation from the positions of deputy director and acting director of the custody department. In addition to instructing the general secretary to handle the handover, I will not be responsible for any departmental affairs from the eighth day of this month. My request is sincere and unavoidable. I hope that the esteemed association will approve it. I am deeply grateful. This is addressed to the Standing Committee."

Reader Communications

A Message to All Readers 158

Key Points of Military Training

Many readers have sent letters asking about military training methods, and some have expressed their opinions on military training. A certain military expert in Beiping has a very concise and essential talk, which is specially introduced as follows:

(1) Military training can be divided into three groups: 1. High school and university students; 2. Young people in industry and commerce who are willing to receive training; 3. Demarcate areas with clear household registration surveys and pilot conscription. The first and second groups should aim to complete one year of training. In a place like Beiping, it is possible to pilot conscription of 5,000 people. If it continues for two years, 20,000 elite soldiers can be obtained.

(2) School military training should be conducted for two hours a day and should be continuous and uninterrupted. Morning training is not as good as evening training. Evening exercises can practice night combat. Training in the field is better than on the training ground. It is best to study during the day and drill in the evening.

(3) It is not necessary to use guns during training. It is a big mistake to say that training cannot be done without guns. In ordinary combat, artillery is used beyond 600 meters, and rifles are used above 300 meters and below 600 meters. The effectiveness of rifles is very small. During the European War, in addition to artillery, the final victory or defeat was determined entirely in a melee. If you can train your body well and use knives and guns, and the short blades are connected, if I stab the enemy to death and the enemy stabs me only to injure me, then I win. Do not say that there may not be many rifles in the future, even if there are guns, they may not all be available. Therefore, the emphasis is on learning fighting skills and training the body. Actions must be agile and strong. This level of relationship is very important.

(4) Moreover, the most taboo is to use rifles in night combat. The sound of the gun is tantamount to telling the enemy where you are. Therefore, melee combat is mostly at night, but mostly not in the wild. At this time, student training must be in the evening, not only for time economy (does not hinder reading), but also to train eyesight (the more you practice at night, the clearer your eyes will be). In the future, when a real war starts, the enemy has artillery and aircraft, and we cannot resist, but when the two armies are close, having melee skills is enough to make the enemy's artillery, aircraft, and rifles completely lose their effectiveness.

(5) Not only is outdoor training very important, but it is also very important to train hard in heavy fog and heavy rain. Students who aspire to save the country, if they cannot endure such hardship, then there is no hope. People who run military training also have no hope if they do not understand this.

(6) Therefore, the best way to run military training now is to run it "alive", not "dead". It takes a lot of effort to run it dead, and it may not be pleasing. Running it alive can achieve twice the result with half the effort.

(7) The general habit of students now is to like listening to military science courses. This is a sign of laziness. Military science is what military officers need, not what soldiers need. The purpose of military training is first to cultivate the majority of good soldiers, and second to cultivate good junior officers. If everyone wants to be a military officer, then military training will definitely fail.

Place of Sadness 161

— Chi Fo

The Sino-Japanese War of Jiawu. The Qing court ordered Li Hongzhang to negotiate peace with Japan. Indemnities and cessions were a great national humiliation. The place of the peace talks was the Shunpanro restaurant in Shimonoseki, Japan. Therefore, it was named the Treaty of Shimonoseki. Wu Zhiqi, a literary giant from Tongcheng, traveled to Japan and happened to pass by the place. He then inscribed a plaque on the Shunpanro: "Place of Sadness." General Wu Baochu, father of the poet Wu Yanfu, also wrote a poem: "Ten thousand acres of clouds stand on the beach. The sea breeze is vast and the white gulls are leisurely. The boatman does not know the place of sadness. He only points to the future, which is Shimonoseki." Now, the violent Japanese invade the border. The three northeastern provinces have fallen into the land trampled by the Japanese slaves. How can the sadness be greater than this? Alas.

Do Not Remove the Garden Grass Zhaifu's Talks

Franklin (6) 162

One of the Apprentice Biographies

Franklin himself and his young son flew that immortal kite in Philadelphia in June of the following year, 1752. This kite is worth describing. Most people only know that Franklin flying a kite was the first time humans took electricity from the sky to the ground, but in fact, this was the second time. The pioneers who took electricity from the sky were Darbari and De Law, and Franklin was their commander-in-chief. Flying a kite was Franklin's personal battle against the sky. Franklin's kite itself was made of a wooden frame and silk: a sharp metal wire was inserted into the wooden frame, and a copper key and a ribbon were tied to the lower end of the double-strand rope. The kite was put into the clouds, and the hand held the ribbon and stood in the doorway to prevent the ribbon from getting wet from the rain. Soon, the loose yarn of the double-strand rope stood up angrily like a wild boar's thorn, the fingers could attract each other, and the finger bones touched the key and sparks flew. He also led the lightning down and stored it in the Leyden jar, proving that its operation was no different from frictional electricity. According to modern electrical theory, Franklin was too close to the copper key while holding the ribbon and would have been electrocuted to death. To do this experiment, people have to be far away. Fourteen months later, a physicist in St. Petersburg, Russia, used an iron rod to take electricity from the sky. He was electrocuted to death by a ball of blue fire when he approached the electrometer. The reason why Franklin did not die was probably because there was only a small amount of lightning on the day he flew the kite. He was truly lucky! Otherwise, Franklin would have sacrificed his life for science.

Franklin was a versatile man. He only had nine years of scientific research, and he contributed to the world with stoves, lightning rods, ether light wave theory, magnetic copper plate printing, printing presses, bifocal glasses, alarm clocks, and his electrical theory. According to himself, his experiments benefited a lot from the craft visits during his apprenticeship. This kind of intimate craft visit for choosing a career was a major invention of his father, a candle and soap maker, in children's education. (The end) (This time, because there was too much to say about national affairs, this biography was interrupted for a long time, and I am deeply sorry.)

Two Brief Biographies 163

— Wang Maichang

Jian Dashi was a native of Taiwan. Or it is said that he was a native of Fujian who lived in Taiwan. He and his younger brother, Dadu, were both known for their chivalry and courage. He could understand the great meaning by reading and admired the theory of equality. He bowed and yielded even to the common people, as if they were honored guests. He especially liked to talk about loyalty and righteousness. He was born in the age of uncle, and he painfully felt the urgency of foreign insults. He often lamented and could not help himself. Looking around, he wept generously and wanted to die for the country. He once traveled to Xiamen and saw a Westerner bullying and humiliating our people. Some people stood by and watched with smug expressions. Dashi stepped forward and slapped his cheek, saying, "Why are you unaware and sigh at the humiliation of your compatriots?" He faced the Westerner with an iron face. The Westerner was shocked and quickly ran away. In the twenty-first year of Guangxu, we ceded Taiwan to the Japanese. Dashi was furious, almost mad. He vowed not to yield to the Japanese. He and Dadu destroyed their homes and recruited warriors, forming an army. After a year of hard fighting, they were finally defeated. They fled to Quanzhou. The Japanese feared him and coerced our officials to demand him urgently. The officials captured him. He cried and said, "What crime have I committed to die? Even if I am guilty, I will die by the laws of the country. I will not hate death. Why do you want to give me to the thieves to kill me? My eyes will never close." The officials gave him to the Japanese after all. The Japanese respected his righteousness and called him a martyr. They wanted to surrender him. Dashi glared and cursed loudly, his hair standing on end. He finally died unyielding. A month after his death, Dadu regrouped the remnants and fought against the Japanese. He was also defeated and died.

The unofficial historian said: "How heroic are the two Jian brothers! In a place where there was nothing that could be done, they knew that it could not be done but still did it to the end. Although their bodies are dead, their spirit of loyalty and righteousness should be rubbed between the two worlds and cannot be extinguished for thousands of years. Later, there will inevitably be those who hear their name and rise up. Then, although their bodies are dead, they may not die. Although the country is destroyed, it may not be destroyed. However, now there are places where things can be done, times when things can be done, but why are they not done? As I write about the two Jian brothers, I cannot help but feel my blood boiling and my hair standing on end. Alas."

World Short News 164

— Hai Ke

Unheard of Super Cat Recently, a very interesting piece of news has been spreading in the world's scientific community. It is that Soviet scientists are studying diligently, wanting to make a domestic animal that can combine the best qualities of sheep, goats, and cows. If this matter can be successfully tested, then it will be easier to mix the worst qualities of the three animals together. However, grafting has been done in the plant world, which is no longer new. Even in the animal world, new species are sometimes discovered. A doctor in Paris is engaged in the study of rats. In order to eliminate rats, he has specially raised a super cat that is larger and more ferocious than ordinary cats. It can kill a large number of rats within a specified time. This matter has now been successfully tested. However, according to some people, this super cat should not be promoted. Ordinary cats already contain a trace of wildness. When wildness breaks out, it is very scary. If a super cat is raised, then it will not only kill a large number of rats, but may also be harmful to humans.

Youth Support-Horse Corps 165

— Bi Bo

With a mere few thousand Japanese pirates, they extinguished our Liaoning and Jilin in an instant. Two hundred thousand troops retreated to preserve their strength, a move called non-resistance, hoping for pity from imperialists. Alas, this shame! I fear such a record is without precedent in history, ancient or modern.

General Ma Zhanshan, understanding his responsibility to defend the territory, vowed to resist to the death and defend Heilongjiang Province. With a single division, though morale was high, it was bound to be defeated against such a strong enemy. Indeed, in less than half a month, it was reported that he abandoned Heihe due to exhausted ammunition and lack of reinforcements. Upon hearing this, the people could not help but weep blood and wring their hearts. Young patriots, unable to bear the demise of their motherland, gathered comrades, numbering several hundred, determined to go to Heihe to assist the isolated army and bring glory to the nation. On the afternoon of the sixth, they held a farewell meeting at the North Station, asking a friend to film a commemorative video for posterity. The speeches at the time were so poignant that everyone wept uncontrollably. Those who donated to help were only common people. The amount was so meager that it was difficult to sustain. I truly do not know if the wealthy can live peacefully after the country is destroyed and the family ruined.

As the brave men bid a heroic farewell, blowing their horns and boarding the train, my heart was heavy. The more I thought about it, the more ashamed I felt. Ashamed of my cowardice, I could not sacrifice myself to follow them, merely offering a pittance. This is hardly enough to atone for my sin of fearing death.

However, those dear compatriots who vowed to die together are all empty-handed, some wearing only thin clothes. The bitter cold of the north will surely cause them to die of cold before they die in battle. This is lamentable! I now respectfully ask all enthusiastic people to actively contribute to these hundreds of enlightened compatriots who are sacrificing themselves for the country, in order to fulfill their loyal and courageous aspirations. My wish is not extravagant, but to contribute what you can.

In the evening, I returned home and told my family what I had seen. My wife and children were moved to tears and offered the earnings from their needlework, asking me to pass them on for assistance. I believe that once this article is published, all those with a conscience will surely be willing to economize on food and clothing to provide a steady stream of aid.

Alas! As I write this article, my heart aches, my tears are dry. My body is still here, but my soul has already gone with those patriotic comrades.

(The fee for this article is designated to be given to Mr. Tan Bozhi of the Sichuan Road Youth Association to be forwarded to the Economic Committee of the Youth Volunteer Corps to Northeast to support Ma.)

Records of What I Saw and Heard in the Old Capital 166

— Zhu An

The Yangshi Lei Family

In the seventh year of the Republic of China, Zhu Qiqian, as an envoy to Nanjing, saw a manuscript in the library titled "Yingzao Fashi" written by Li Jie of the Song Dynasty. He immediately took it and praised it, and had it printed. Thus, people gradually began to learn that our country had such an architectural scholar eight hundred years ago, who bequeathed to posterity engineering methods that had never been written down in books. Although the Northern Song Dynasty, when Li Jie lived, was already an era of decline in architecture, the styles inherited from the Song and Ming dynasties could still be traced back to their origins, making it an extremely valuable document. Later, because the images in the book were incomplete and insufficient to provide proof, he extensively searched for the two existing copies in the Siku Quanshu, compared and supplemented them. He entrusted Tao Xiang and Guo Baochang to manage the matter, and in the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, a large-character version with meticulous revisions was published. The colors in the colored illustrations were superimposed and blended, fresh and dazzling. It is now sold by the Commercial Press, priced at more than seventy yuan. Zhu Qiqian studied ancient and modern architecture for decades. In the early years of the Republic of China, many new buildings in Beijing, such as Zhengyangmen, the Wenhua and Wuying Halls, and Zhongshan Park, were all designed by Zhu Qiqian, blending the old and the new, all with elegant designs, praised by Chinese and foreigners alike. To this day, Zhu Qiqian is credited with giving Beiping the scale of a modern capital. In the eighteenth year of the Republic of China, Zhu Qiqian exhibited the drawings and models he had collected over the years at Zhongshan Park. The following year, with the support of the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture, he established the Society for Research in Chinese Architecture in Beiping, publishing a quarterly journal four times a year and holding exhibitions of achievements from time to time. The most interesting was the exhibition of Yuanmingyuan relics held in March of the twentieth year. The motivation for this exhibition was the joint purchase of Yangshi Lei models with the Beiping Library in the nineteenth year. The Yangshi Lei family were hereditary engineers who undertook the construction of palaces and mausoleums. Major national projects had to be obtained from them, so their family had thousands of drawings of major projects since the Jiaqing and Daoguang eras. When Zhu Qiqian was Minister of the Interior, he heard of their name and sought them out. The Lei family avoided meeting him. In recent years, forced by livelihood, they began to peddle their treasures everywhere. The treasures accumulated over generations were in danger of being scattered. Therefore, the Beiping Library spent money to buy them all, costing about six or seven thousand yuan. Among them, there were more than 1,800 drawings and 18 models related to the Yuanmingyuan. This matter caused a sensation for a time, and scholars were eager to see them first. Among the Yuanmingyuan documents, the most noteworthy to Chinese and foreigners are the twenty drawings of the waterworks of the Xiyang Lou in the Harmonious Wonder Garden. These drawings are Qianlong copperplate prints. The existing ones are stored in the Beiping Palace Museum and the Rehe Imperial Palaces in Liaoning. The original prints collected by old families in Beiping are consistent with the images in the "Study of the Beijing Imperial Palace" by Siren and the "Complete Collection of World Art in Japan." Compared with the current state of ruins, it is even more unbearable to witness. Seventy years have passed since the Yuanmingyuan was destroyed. Those who have seen its heyday are almost non-existent. Therefore, the fact that the garden extensively adopted Western architecture is hardly known. Those who wrote travelogues and poems in the past did not pay much attention to this. Recently, scholars have combined Chinese and Western records and determined that Westerners participated in determining the drawings at that time. Alas, wild grasses in the setting sun, broken tiles and scattered beams. How much blood and tears of our ancestors are stored in this place! How can posterity not keep this in mind and use it as a warning?

The Expenses of Charlie Chaplin's Sons 167

— Yan Ming

A report from Lita Grey Chaplin, Charlie Chaplin's ex-wife, has recently been submitted to the court, indicating that the expenses for Charlie Chaplin's two sons last year seem to have decreased slightly compared to the previous year. His two sons are named Charles Chaplin Jr., who is nine years old this year, and Sydney, who is eight years old this year. When the comedic star divorced his ex-wife, he agreed to pay each son $6,000 in annual education and upbringing expenses.

For the past year, ending at the end of September, Charles Chaplin Jr. spent a total of $3,676, and Sydney spent a total of $3,509. These amounts include a monthly accommodation fee of $200 and the wages of a nanny. In the previous year, Charles Chaplin Jr. spent $3,619, and Sydney spent $3,638. Comparatively, the expenses have slightly decreased.

Currently, Charles Chaplin Jr. has accumulated $8,730 from his education and upbringing expenses, while Sydney has $8,886. The two brothers each wear five pairs of leather shoes a year, priced from $1.25 to $8. The older brother's total shoe expenses for the year were $26, while the younger brother's were $24. As for clothing, Charles Chaplin Jr.'s expenses were $528, while Sydney's were $540.

Charles Chaplin Jr.'s toys were only worth $1.20, which is rare among children. His expenses were mostly used for medical care, nursing, and miscellaneous expenses.

The Rotary Club of Storytellers

Sharing the Enemy with Our Children (6) 169

— Gu Mingdao

Chapter One: The Drums of Yuyang

The troops of the Land of the Rising Sun rushed to the school gate, preparing for resistance from the students. They first set up two machine guns and then shouted loudly, bursting in. At this moment, it was as if a large gang of robbers had arrived, searching in all directions. They quickly arrested Principal Xiong Feng and sent him to their headquarters. Most of the students had already hidden. A few were taken prisoner. Two Rising Sun soldiers rushed to the girls' dormitory to search, like hunting dogs, eager to devour. At this moment, in dormitory number ten, there was a girl, about twenty years old, her delicate jade face flushed with a pale color. She was tightly barricading the door with tables and chairs. But the cunning Rising Sun soldiers seemed to already know that their target was inside. They hurriedly knocked on the door with their gun butts. After a few blows, the door collapsed. Two Rising Sun soldiers jumped into the room from the tables, looking at the girl cowering in a corner. They couldn't help but reveal a smug look on their faces, walking towards the girl, speaking in Chinese: "Little girl, don't panic. We are here to protect you. As long as you are agreeable and can give us some fun, we guarantee your life will be safe." Saying that, they moved closer step by step. The girl was like a fawn waiting to die, about to meet the ravenous mouths of tigers and wolves, and the two Rising Sun soldiers were like two devils, opening their bloody mouths, wanting to swallow this flower-like and jade-like female student. But at this critical moment for the girl, with no chance of escape, her panicked expression suddenly turned into a stern attitude. Her body no longer retreated, standing upright, her eyes wide open, scolding them, "Dogs! Inhuman bandits! I would rather die! Who dares to violate me!" As she spoke, she had an air of inviolability. One of the Rising Sun soldiers was somewhat stunned to see her like this. But the other Rising Sun soldier grinned evilly. "Good. You're cursing people. You want to die? I won't let you die." As he spoke, he pounced on the girl, wanting to grab her. The girl had no defense. Coincidentally, there was an ink bottle on the windowsill behind her. The girl quickly grabbed it in her hand and threw it at the Rising Sun soldier's face, hitting his nose directly, breaking his nose and causing blood to flow, splashing his face with ink. He couldn't help but become enraged. He raised his pistol, wanting to shoot the girl. Just then, with a bang, a figure fell backward.

Changes in Silver Prices and Exchange Rates 173

Since September 21st, the Shanghai exchange market has presented a new atmosphere, and the value of currency has changed suddenly. The increase in silver prices and British pounds has been affected by the UK's abolition of the gold standard. However, the rise in silver prices and the US dollar is more complex. The future changes will be a major issue for us to pay attention to. Before September 21st of this year, the New York silver market price was consistently around 27.75 cents per ounce. After the news of the UK's abolition of the gold standard spread to the New World, it suddenly rose to 29.25 cents. Most speculators bought large amounts of raw silver, hoping that the UK would restore the complex standard system. Therefore, in four days, it rose to 31 cents. The local silver price and US dollar also rose accordingly. However, the facts were the opposite. The UK did not need raw silver, and the decline resumed, falling to 27.25 cents, which was weaker than the market price before September 21st. The comparison between silver and the US dollar is based on the high and low of the New York silver market price. However, after mid-October, it reversed and there was no correct way to find it. Raw silver speculators shifted their focus and no longer paid attention to the comparison between gold and silver. In the first week of November, raw silver trading became more frequent. According to general speculation, the United States and countries related to the East are fighting for the international silver market. Therefore, the amount of transactions broke the silver market record in recent years. In the days from October 29th to November 10th, the price of raw silver rose by a quarter. However, the comparison between the US dollar and silver did not rise sharply. After the reaction started, the strength of the decline was the same as the rise. Therefore, in the eight days from November 10th, the price of October 29th was restored, which was close to the price before September 21st. Therefore, the comparison between the US dollar and silver also fell to the same level as before the rise. When the price of silver and other countries' currencies is higher, most people exchange silver coins for gold coins from other countries. However, the savings of banks in Shanghai and other ports remain the same. In mid-October, there was a high price. Shanghai is the trade center of the country and the only port for foreign trade. The amount of goods imported and exported is very huge. Therefore, this silver price change and its financial independence have little impact. Recently, Shanghai has repeatedly transported huge amounts of silver to various places and has pre-shipped the full amount of silver before the port closes, in order to adjust the winter finances of northern China. In short, Shanghai is a major industrial and commercial port, and its greatness will not change due to external influences.

Yesterday, at the Chinese Securities Exchange, the bond market situation was as follows: one-month futures still had no trading activity, and December futures remained quite quiet. The enthusiasm of buyers and sellers was still sporadic. Spot trading continued to be lively, with various opening prices in the early and late markets. The stronger trend of Disbandment Bonds was probably due to the expectation of lottery-based principal repayment soon, which increased market demand for them. It is estimated that the total spot trading volume for the day was 23,000 yuan, with futures trading volume reaching over 1.6 million yuan in the morning and over 1.4 million yuan in the afternoon, totaling only 3.07 million yuan.

Sudden Rise in the Oil and Asphalt Market 184

Oversold… Rebound Also Strong

The asphalt market rose too much between spring and summer, so the new goods were not seen and then the price fell sharply. However, the fall was also too much, so-called “when things reach an extreme, they revert.” The initial price of new goods of hemp oil from Macheng (麻城) of Hankou this time was only 15 taels and 6 qian. Compared with the old oil which was sold for 32 or 33 taels two months ago, it has fallen by almost half, which is really unbelievable. However, after this fall, both dealers and producers believe that the time has come, and they are all starting to bid. However, there are not many new goods available, so can there be such a huge supply, which has led to a turnaround. According to yesterday's Hankou telegram, it has opened at 17 taels and is now at 18 taels. However, this winter's candle manufacturers did not prepare much stock in advance due to the high price of old oil, and they have been gradually decreasing prices before the new oil arrived, so they did not dare to prepare winter goods immediately. Therefore, the base stocks are very thin. When the market turnaround was seen, they began to purchase goods from various places, but the trend had already risen. Moreover, Jingyou oil (荆油) in Hankou usually arrives after the winter solstice, and even if it is shipped early, it will be a small amount. Fortunately, you are competing with me for it, and it is not enough to allocate, so the Hankou market has been in a state of short supply for several days. Local dealers have telegraphed to purchase, but there are no spot goods available, and only one or two out of ten can be purchased. Moreover, the inventory was not prepared due to the sharp fall after the new goods were released, so the total market stock is less than 2,000 pieces, which is rare for the new goods to be launched with such a thin stock. It is reported that the market in Jinlan, Zhejiang has also risen by two or three yuan. The price of car oil in Jiaxing is rising even more sharply because many have already been sold. It is said that the price of delivered car has been sold to 30 yuan, and the car delivered may require about 32 yuan.

Automobile News Special Article

The 1932 Model New Car "Standard" Will Soon Arrive in Shanghai 187

Time flies. In the blink of an eye, 1931 is about to bid us a sad farewell. And 1932 will soon meet us. At this time of year, car factories in Europe and the United States are busy planning or manufacturing the 1932 model new cars. And some manufacturers have already released new cars. According to the latest news, these new cars will soon be shipped to Shanghai and publicly exhibited. Now, let us describe the advantages of the first batch of new "Standard" cars to arrive in Shanghai, which I think will also be welcome news for readers.

Key Advantages that are Economical and Meet Standards. The "Standard" car has been around for twenty-eight years. Therefore, this year's new car is a crystallization of the experience gained over the past twenty-eight years. The money spent in the beginning of planning and construction is more than just ten thousand pounds. In addition, engineers and ordinary workers have spent a lot of brainpower over the years to produce the 1932 model new car. This new car will surprise us at first sight, because its main advantage is that it meets the principles of economy and is very comfortable to drive. However, the selling price is low, and the cost of driving is extremely economical. Strictly speaking, the results of the new cars produced by various British factories in the past have never been so good. Car owners can be very satisfied after purchasing this new car. In terms of recent social aspects, culture is advancing day by day, and the appearance of the required cars is also an important issue. This 1932 model "Standard" car is also as beautiful as possible in terms of form. In terms of the types of new cars, there are four types: No. 20, No. 16, Big No. 9 and Small No. 9.

A Leader in Low-Priced Cars. Once we buy this new car, we can know that its internal structure has some advantages. In the past, only high-priced cars had them. Low-priced cars must not be so beautiful. For example, the fuel tank is placed at the rear, which is very safe. Semi-elliptical springs and shock absorbers are installed on the front and rear parts. Magna-style wheels and shatterproof glass windscreens have always been unique to high-priced cars. However, the 1932 model "Standard" car is equipped with the above-mentioned various devices, and the selling price is still low. Is this not a successful product and sufficient to meet the needs of society?

Extremely Fuel Efficient When Driving. Not only that, but the "Standard" car paid special attention to the economy of gasoline when it was manufactured. Therefore, the consumption of fuel is incomparable to any other car when driving. At the same time, the safety and the ability to travel on the road have not been reduced in the slightest.

Convenient Driving and Comfortable Handling. In addition to the economy of gasoline, the "Standard" new car is also satisfactory in terms of convenient driving and comfortable handling. Car owners can easily prove it after purchasing it. Therefore, "Standard" cars are most suitable for women to drive. In a nutshell, the "Standard" new car is light, smooth, simple and convenient to drive, and the handling is easy. The braking power is strong and the braking is convenient, which makes the driver satisfied everywhere.

Beautiful Car Body and Unique Style. When the owner of the "Standard" new car drives out, there is absolutely no restriction in the car. Even on rough and uneven roads, there is no need to worry about shaking. Therefore, there is no need to worry about all explosions and ruptures. Therefore, the car body of the "Standard" new car is made by famous craftsmen, and safety issues are taken care of everywhere. All "Standard" new cars have car bodies made of steel plates, and the four car doors are inlaid with artificial ivory, which is especially pleasing to the eye. Therefore, the structure of the new car is not only excellent in terms of mechanical parts, but also greatly improved in terms of the car body.

Four-Part Speed, No Noise At All. When this new car is driving on the road, its various advantages are even more amazing. When driving on ordinary roads, it is only necessary to use the second gear, and the highest gear also has special advantages. The gears are divided into four-part speed, and there is no noise at all when using the third gear, which is especially excellent. If a three-part speed gearbox is used, the second gear will not make even the slightest noise.

New Method of Heat Reduction. The heat reduction device is completely manufactured using a new method, and the appearance is even more impressive. This is also a special advantage of the "Standard" new car. The stripes painted on the outside are quite beautiful. When people see it today, they will know that the new car has special advantages and is very comfortable to drive.

New Car Top is Convenient to Open and Close. According to the manufacturers of the "Standard" new car, the 1932 model new car can be used for two purposes. When driving out, if the people sitting in the car want to protect themselves from the wind and rain, they can close the car top tightly, which is no different from a sedan. However, if you want the sun to shine in or the air to be fresh, you can remove the car top or a convertible car. Therefore, all 1932 model "Standard" new cars use Stanlite Sliding Roof (斯丹立脫斜形車頂), and the car top is very convenient and quick to open and close. It can also be opened and closed at any time while driving. Car owners will know the convenience of this car top once they buy it.

It is said that these new cars will be displayed in the model room at No. 702 Jing'an Temple Road after they arrive in Shanghai. At that time, people in Shanghai who want to buy cars can go and have a look.

Citroen's American Visit - A Fragment of Mr. Citroen's Success Story 188

André Citroen, hailed as the "Henry Ford of France," recently embarked on a journey from France to visit major automobile manufacturers in America. During his time in the US, he meticulously inspected various renowned car factories. Consequently, his American hosts harbored a shared sentiment, wondering what insights Citroen would incorporate into his vehicles upon returning to France. In 1912, this French automotive magnate traveled to America, adopting American mass production methods. After returning to France, he immediately put them into practice, leading to a substantial increase in car production. In 1923, Citroen revisited America, gaining even more valuable knowledge. Upon his return, he was laden with insights, implementing everything he had learned in America into his factory. As a result, Citroen's production leaped to 200 vehicles per day. Regarding his latest trip, commentators suggest that Citroen harbors even grander ambitions and will undoubtedly gain even more. He purportedly intends to establish a Citroen branch factory in America.

Despite Citroen's moniker as the "Henry Ford of France," his daily life differs significantly from Ford's. Citroen's parents were quite wealthy, distinguishing him from Ford. He received considerable education in mechanical engineering in his early years. Although already 54 years old, he is short, energetic, and lively, with sparse hair and a radiant demeanor. The spectacles perched on his nose and his piercing gaze immediately reveal him as a man of talent and intellect.

When Citroen began his business, his factory initially produced gear machinery. Later, he transitioned to manufacturing automobiles. With the outbreak of the Great War, he enlisted in the military to serve his country, working in a front-line engineering unit for six months. The government highly valued Citroen's assistance and appointed him to establish a munitions factory for producing artillery shells in a short time. The factory was completed in five months, producing countless shells. Until the war's end, this factory produced 50,000 shells daily. Citroen, realizing the war would not last forever, decided to convert the shell factory into an automobile manufacturing plant. In March 1919, the shell factory ceased operations, and by July of the same year, the Citroen automobile factory was completed. From then on, the armaments factory, which had specialized in producing lethal weapons, was transformed into an automobile factory that benefited humanity. Citroen's foresight and vision are truly commendable.

Citroen's adventurous endeavors are akin to gambling, yet his automobile factory is undoubtedly a winning bet. He is also an avid gambler in games of chance. On one occasion in Deauville, Citroen won $700,000. In another instance, he lost $400,000 in a card game. However, after this loss, his banker advised him to cease gambling to preserve his business. Citroen complied, focusing on the automobile manufacturing business. Today, he can produce 100,000 vehicles annually, encompassing various sizes and types, including four-cylinder and six-cylinder models, with prices starting from $900 per vehicle. Citroen's business methods are highly praised, and he is regarded as an American-style businessman among Europeans. He has employed various advertising strategies to attract customers. The ingenuity of his designs surpasses even that of famous American advertising professionals. The most renowned and impressive of his advertisements was renting the Eiffel Tower in Paris as an advertising space. This tower, known as the Eiffel Tower, is a world-famous tall structure. After renting the advertising space, Citroen adorned it with electric lights spelling out "Citroen," clearly highlighting the advantages of his products, attracting significant attention. Another grand undertaking with advertising qualities, although not direct advertising, achieved the same level of attention as the Eiffel Tower advertisement. What was this advertisement? It was Citroen's automobiles being the first to cross the Sahara Desert. Citroen automobiles traversed the desert, starting from Algeria and ending in Timbuktu, a distance of 3,000 miles. Citroen's engineers installed rubber underlays on the wheels, enabling them to traverse the desert terrain, much like military tanks equipped with metal underlays.

Besides the Javel quai, Citroen's automobile factory also has five branch factories. Each factory is large in scale, employing 4,000 workers. His factories can produce 300 vehicles daily. Compared to the production numbers of American automobile factories, this number may seem limited, but within France, Citroen is undoubtedly the largest. His production accounts for 20 percent of the nation's total.

A well-known anecdote about Citroen is often praised, revealing his character. A young boy in France once wrote to Citroen, stating that he excelled in both academics and conduct at home and school. He had saved two small silver coins given to him by his father as pocket money. The boy continued, stating that he wished to purchase a Citroen automobile with these two small silver coins. Citroen was delighted upon receiving the letter and replied, inviting the boy to visit. Upon the boy's arrival, Citroen guided him through the automobile showroom, encouraging him to choose any car he desired. After careful consideration, the boy suddenly said to Citroen, "No, having seen these automobiles, I have decided to keep my two small silver coins."

A Record of the Summer Peck International Auto Show (Continued) - Yingdai 189

The installation of shock absorbers has become a commonplace event; every vehicle has them. In terms of braking, significant improvements have been made. Safety glass is equipped in vehicles of all sizes. At least ten companies at the Xia Ling Pei exhibition display vehicles equipped with above-standard shatterproof glass. Such as Luer Luis, Lawyer Ma, Austin, and Lilan. For the convenience of driving at night and to prevent accidents, the new cars this year mostly adopt light-avoidance methods. Therefore, the 1932 Luxkleve headlights are installed. This type of headlight contains two bundles of filaments, which can be arbitrarily made to emit ordinary light or avoid dazzling light. The glass in front of the light is also a specially made product. There are many oblique concave surfaces, so that the light is obliquely refracted, and the road is clearer. For this reason, accidents are also less likely to occur. The taillight displayed by the Gilbert Company can emit strong light in an instant to attract the attention of drivers behind, which is much more economical than long-term bright taillights. As for the structure of the car body, it will be described in the following text.

The success of small cars - The Thailing Fuda No. 7 car has had considerable success since its introduction. Overseas Automotive News - Pei 190

A new Ford factory is established in the UK. The American Ford Motor Company is a leader in the world's automobile manufacturing industry. Recently, it has re-focused on the development of overseas businesses. In addition to the Detroit headquarters factory, branch factories are set up in various important areas to produce Ford cars for local application. Its British branch factory has been established, and the factory site is on the banks of the River Thames, about eighteen miles from London, the capital of England, with the place name Daqin Hamu. The Ford cars required by the European market in the future will be manufactured by this factory. The scale of the Ford Motor Company in England is very large. In addition to the major automobile factories in the United States, this factory should be the largest in the world. The Daqin Hamu factory site is very large, covering 110 acres, with another 484 acres of surplus land for expansion. The front of the factory is about half a mile away from the River Thames. This open space can be used to store raw materials, and the manufactured cars can also be loaded onto ships or trains from here and transported to other places. The equipment in the factory is also considerable. The manufacturing workshop and the housing for the configuration workshop are 1,000 feet long and 300 feet wide. The wide field between the two houses is 80 feet wide and covered. Driving track cars. The furnace weighs 500 tons, which is the largest in southern England. The siliconizing machine also weighs 500 tons. There are forty-five byproduct coke ovens, which can carbonize 800 tons of coal per day.

Current situation of the American automobile market. From October to December

It is the last quarter of the automobile market in a year. Experienced American automobile manufacturers often call this time the season of waiting and seeing, because customers often wait and see at this time. Probably the new cars of next year will often be found on the market at the end of a year. Therefore, customers often do not buy immediately, but wait for all the cars to come out before purchasing and selecting. Judging from the current situation, although there are signs of stagnation in the market, it will soon be eliminated, because most customers cannot wait for long and will eventually choose to buy a car. Generally, a car is used for at least one or two years, and up to three years. Car owners must have the intention to replace new cars. Therefore, filling old cars is also an important development of the automobile market. For example, 6,000,000 new cars were sold in 1929, so this old car will inevitably be discarded next year and replaced with a new car instead. As for the manufacturers, they often urge car owners to replace new cars at this time, and offset the price with their old cars. For this reason, at the time of alternation between new and old, both sellers and buyers have a waiting and seeing phenomenon. As for selling cars, it is easier to sell them to people who already have cars. If the use of automobiles is a kind of plaything for the rich, it will be very difficult to sell cars to people with this kind of psychology. Therefore, the trend of automobile sales today is actually easier than in the past. Compared with ten years ago, the difference is even greater. At that time, 9,000,000 cars were sold, and there were still many people who had not had the opportunity to drive a car. In 1921, about 1.5 million cars were sold. So everyone felt worried that the market was oversaturated. However, in a few years, automobile manufacturers shouted the slogan "one car per family". It is estimated that there are 25,000,000 families in total. After that, this thing was really realized. Then they changed their slogan to "every person in the family must have a car." From then on, the scope of selling cars became even wider.
