Road Administration Studies Move in Shaanxi and Sichuan Provinces 191

Shaanxi and Sichuan provinces are located in the remote northwest. If you want to facilitate transportation, it is not enough to build roads for automobile traffic to communicate with each other and achieve balanced development. Therefore, the authorities of the two provinces also know that the mountains and rivers are difficult to repair, and the stagnation of goods is not a way to develop real industries and

Benefit merchants, not a way to advance culture and facilitate exchange. Therefore, each province has carefully planned the road administration of its own province and carefully repaired it. Now the information obtained from the investigation is recorded as follows.

Road Construction Plan of Shaanxi Province The Highway Bureau of Shaanxi Province has specially formulated a concrete plan for the recent north-south trunk line and the progress in order to develop transportation to meet the needs of the day. The main points are: (1) Bao Nan Auto Road The road is from Bao Lin to Han Nan. Strive to start construction as soon as possible within the shortest possible time. All the survey engineers in the county have been properly assigned. Once the provincial government's administrative meeting approves the concrete plan, they will immediately take action to rush the repair. Before the construction of the road is started, it is planned to send personnel to Baoji first, and rush to complete the project from Bao Lin to Fengxiang in order to meet the needs of transporting materials in the future. (2) Xi Tong Light Rail. This road from Xi'an to Tongzhou was planned to be put into operation for a long time. Only the western section of the Longhai Road still needs to be borrowed, which has not been carried out. Now it has been negotiated with the Longhai authorities, and they will go to Chongbao to pick up and transport it, and set a time limit for laying it down. All earthwork matters on this road are also being actively carried out and will soon be completed. (3) Wei North Transportation. The two automobile roads in Wei North, Xi Chao (Xi'an to Chaoyi) and Xi Chang (Xi'an to Changwu), used to be located in Chang'an, which was inconvenient for merchants. It is now planned to connect the two lines of Xi Chang Xi Chao through Yang Yu Li Quan Du. In the future, merchants traveling on the road in Wei North can arrive in Chang from Chao in case of emergency, without having to detour through Xi'an. (4) East-West Thoroughfare. Recently, there have been many damages to the east-west automobile road due to yin and rain. In addition to expanding the Bureau's engineering team as appropriate and assigning cadres to actively protect and repair the automobile administration, construction bureaus in various counties have been strictly ordered to organize engineering teams within the specified time to rush to build the automobile roads within their respective counties to facilitate commercial transportation. At the same time, the road protection teams on each road were also ordered that if there are larger projects in a certain place that urgently need to be built, they should immediately report to the Provincial Bureau so that personnel can be sent to rush the repair. The overall goal is to facilitate passengers.

Roads throughout Sichuan Province. In recent years, the construction of roads in various counties and cities in Sichuan has lacked statistics. The 20 roads that have already been open to traffic and are still under construction are: (1) Yu Wan Road, from the north bank of Chongqing to Wan County. It has now been repaired from Wan County to the watershed. It has been opened to traffic. From the watershed to Liangshan Dianjiang Changshou to Jiangbei and other counties. After a meeting of the construction bureau chiefs of Liang Dian Chang, it was decided to transfer the short-term loan to be repaid as the cost of continuing construction. And it was decided to follow the Yan Jian Road method, each county built in sections, and the work could be ordered after the transfer of receipt. (2) Cheng Peng Road, from Chengdu Wai North to Peng Hao. It has been opened to traffic. Although it was blocked by the damage of the bridge of this nature, it has now been repaired. (3) He Tong Road, from Hechuan Nanjin Street to Tongliang, is funded by a private enterprise company. The roadbed from Hechuan Yongli has now been measured. The price of Shang Tianzhong Tian Xia Tian is given. Each share is limited to ten yuan. Those who complete the grain in more than three copies can receive a stock certificate. It was decided at the Anju meeting in Tong County on September 4. Construction can start after the autumn harvest is completed. (4) Tong He Road, from Tongnan to Hechuan, was commissioned by Commander Liu Wenhui to Zhao Peisang, the head of the group, as the supervisor. The plan has been confirmed to start construction within the month. It will be repaired from Tongnan to Anju Town. It will meet with He Tong Road. (5) Wei Jing Road, from Weiyuan Zigong City. It has now been completed. Automobiles and rickshaws will soon be driven. (6) Lu Long Road, from Xiaoshi, Luxian to Longchang. The line that meets with Yu Jian Road. It is currently under survey. Construction will start after the survey is completed. The Road Bureau is located in Luxian. (7) Sui Tong Road, from Suining to Tongnan. Automobiles have been open to traffic for a long time. Traffic is still unimpeded as usual. (8) Tongbao Nanlang Section, from Tongchuan to Nanzhang in Baoning via Shehong Yanning. The total length is 285 li. The southern section is 240 li long. The Langzhong section is 45 li. The budget for the southern section is 120,000 yuan. Construction started in November of the 19th year of the Republic of China. The engineer is Zhou Jiwu. The technician is Tan Zhugan. It was interrupted due to the war in Beidao. It is now urging to continue construction. It is expected to be completed and opened to traffic by the end of the year. (9) Chang Hou Road, from Changning County to Houpu. County magistrate Chen Chuxiang advocated the construction of this road in order to connect the county's water and land transportation. It is currently under measurement. (10) Songshi Road, from Songpan to Maoxian. It is more than 300 li long. It is the only transportation line for merchants in western Sichuan. (14) Zi Nei Road, from Zizhong to Neijiang. This road is the central trunk road of the Sheng Yu Line. It is still open to traffic as usual and is unimpeded. (15) Jingfu Road, from Baijing to Fushun. Youth Garden

The Soul of the Nation 192

— Ceng Jinke

People, regardless of age, status, or wealth, have souls; nations, regardless of size, prosperity, or decline, also have souls. People without souls cannot survive, and nations without souls cannot exist. Human souls are divided into good and evil, and so are national souls. However, there are people in the world whose good souls do not receive good results, but there are no nations with good souls that cannot survive, because people can achieve prominence through evil deeds, while nations cannot rely solely on violence to assert their dominance.

What is the soul of a nation? It is national consciousness. Now, in the 20th century, empty words are of no use. Under powerful forces, there is no such thing as justice and righteousness; there is only resistance and struggle. However, resistance and struggle cannot be achieved overnight.

China is a weak nation. This is undeniable. It is certainly difficult to win against an unreasonable Japan with a weak nation. Even now, it seems impossible to resist the violence being inflicted upon us, because the Chinese people, who are "a heap of loose sand," are still "a heap of loose sand." The Chinese people, who are called the "sick men of East Asia," are still "sick men of East Asia." To organize some "sand"-like "sick men" together hastily, with some people just trying to show off, and then say they are going to resist the violent Japan, is at least a ridiculous act. Regarding this point, everyone who has participated in so-called patriotic work is very clear and I need not say more.

However, should we just let Japan invade us?

Of course, we must resist, but empty talk is useless. If our people were like the people of Japan, loving their country as much as their own lives, they would usually pay attention to ways to "defend against insults." The important people in the government are also part of the people, and they were people before they became officials. Of course, they can love the country as one, and through the joint efforts of the people and the government, there must be a way to "strengthen the country." But what about our people? What about our government? This is also clear to everyone and I need not say more. The Japanese people are the opposite of us in their attitude towards their country, and have been painstakingly working hard to become strong for decades. The legacy strategy of the Meiji Restoration, the first step was to conquer Taiwan, the second step was to conquer Korea, and both have already been realized. Now they are going to realize their third step, "to destroy Manchuria and Mongolia in order to conquer the entire territory of China." If we can start from this point to work hard and revitalize, then our nation can still become strong in the future. If we continue to procrastinate and be dispirited, I am afraid that the time of national subjugation is not far away. The soul of a nation is its entire people. From the health of these people, we can know whether the nation is healthy. To seek the health of the nation, we must first seek the health of the people's thoughts and abilities. To seek the health of the people's thoughts and abilities, we must first plan for the popularization and improvement of education, and plant the idea of patriotism in the hearts and minds of every young person, remember it firmly and never forget it, so that every person from childhood to adulthood has the idea of patriotism, and does their best to seek the health of their nation, loving their country as much as their own lives. Then their country will be strong and prosperous. At present, although it is hopeless to strengthen China, even if we do not have the ambition to dominate the world in the future, we should hurry up and cultivate the soul of our nation now for the sake of avoiding destruction in the future—the national consciousness of young people, especially children.

Shanghai Market

Movie Sketches by Lu Mengshu: Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream 193

(I) Introduction

To adapt a literary work that has artistic merit into an extraordinary sound film, after the great success of Remarque's "All Quiet on the Western Front," which can shine in film history alongside it and create a new record, in my personal opinion, it must be Robert Emmett Sherwood's "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream" (Waterloo Bridge, originally translated as "Waterloo Bridge"). Non-war works have never aroused my interest, and non-war films especially make me avoid them like discarding leftovers. It is such a refusal to decay and abandon my long-held advocacy for film that prevented me from introducing "All Quiet on the Western Front," even though it caused a sensation in Shanghai at the time. Of course, a film like "All Quiet on the Western Front" has its greatness and does not need my evaluation. However, my personal subjective conditions for film must be expressed here. I believe that today's China is already rotten inside, riddled with holes, and the environment is stripping, eroding, trampling, and grinding. If there is not a strong "force" in art to resist foreign aggression and pacify internal affairs, to heal decay and treat waste, then the crisis that is about to step on our feet will be more than just the collapse of fences and the loss of territory. Film is a comprehensive art that shifts general will and changes general emotions. Under the current national conditions, it is especially important to use the four characters "courageous and fierce" as the guiding principle for public education, so that the Chinese nation, which is like a plate of loose sand suffering from jaundice, can be reborn, with a "force" of unity, and create a situation where all Chinese men and women on the front of national consciousness are healthy, strong, calm, and brave Qiu Jiu (a fictional strong man). The Qiu Ba (soldiers) of China, as the facts have told us, are unreliable. The superiors only indulge in personal hedonism, while the inferiors only waste food and retreat in battle. However, I must also declare that there is grass everywhere in the world. The Qiu Ba I am talking about does not include General Ma Zhanshan, because General Ma Zhanshan and his group of strong men, in the midst of 200,000 troops, succumbed to the wind, showed great righteousness, resisted Japan with an isolated army, were heroic and robust, brave and loyal, and were indeed the Qiu Ba we most needed. As for the young people who only know how to jump like monkeys and howl like pigs in the peach garden-like Shanghai, but are unwilling to truly prepare for "force," I still say they are not qualified to be Qiu Jiu.

My reasons for abandoning non-war films and my subjective conditions for film are as described above. However, I do not absolutely agree with works of war, but always take it as a prerequisite that it does not lose the inherent mission of film art. If there is a film that is insignificant and discarded by people, but the mission of film art is strongly expressed, I will inevitably recognize it as a work that is beneficial to the world and people's hearts. For example, "All Quiet on the Western Front," although I did not introduce it, I did not express opposition, because it has its greatness, which is the so-called mission of film art. I heard that it has been banned in China. The ban was when Chairman Chiang moved to Nanchang, which was several months ago. I cannot criticize whether such a policy of preventing problems before they occur is appropriate, but I should speak out for "All Quiet on the Western Front" because although it uses non-war as the tip of its theme, it does powerfully and clearly stimulate people's emotions of loving the nation and saving the country in the performance.

Let's get back to the topic. I said above that there is a Qiu Jiu in "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream." Although it does not give us an example of Qiu Jiu to see, the slogan that Chinese youth often hang on their lips, "Save the country without forgetting love, love without forgetting saving the country," is clearly and consciously reflected in it, teaching people how to implement this slogan. Western films, no matter how absurd, crude, or vulgar their themes are, always stand in front of the nation and shoulder their inherent mission. The understanding we gain from enjoying different styles in Western films is that the Western nation is so strong because its solid foundation is not built by a national government in a short period, but is indeed a great achievement of the tireless efforts of artists from ancient times to the present. Rome was not built in a day. Under today's circumstances, we cannot deny that we must expect our Chinese artists. But what about our Chinese artists? Alas, it is so sad to see them.

"Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream" was produced in the same Universal City studio in the United States as "All Quiet on the Western Front." According to Universal Pictures itself, it is the only work after "All Quiet on the Western Front." It is a special achievement and an unusual and compact film. I heard that movie star Douglas Fairbanks also praised it, and the unanimous praise from American movie lovers is especially evidenced by the records in the movie theaters. In short, it is an extraordinary sound film that absolutely does not give people any doubt because it is the result of the hard work of a group of people and not an ordinary product.

Speaking of this group of people, I should introduce them selectively here.

(II) Original Author Robert Emmett Sherwood

First of all, talent is not very reliable. Talent with knowledge and experience is a successful artist. I would like to express my respect for Robert Emmett Sherwood first. Although he is not like other writers who first advertised a prominent name in the literary world, the artistic skills he demonstrates in his works are so superb that it is truly admirable. Do the readers doubt my words? Just take a look at the inner descriptions and scene performances of "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream" and you will understand. You don't even have to calm down and read the original work carefully.

From the perspective of the Chinese, this admirable writer is qualified to be an old man. He was born on April 4, 1896. He is over forty years old. He was born in New Rochelle, New York, USA. He is purely an American. He was talented since childhood. When he grew up, he majored in literature at Harvard University. He was blessed by nature and worked hard, so his attainments were extraordinary. Therefore, his achievements in Harvard were very amazing. After graduation, he devoted himself to cultural undertakings to develop his talent and served as the editor of the drama column of "Vanity Fair" magazine and the social column of "Life" magazine. With the novel selection of materials and the well-organized arrangement, he was very popular among the public. He also published articles from time to time to criticize films and dramas. Soon, he became a critic of drama and film.

Later, as his knowledge and skills increased, he resigned from his editorial position and devoted himself to the creation of drama. His plays, including "The Road to Rome," "The Love Nest," and "The Queen's Husband," all showed his talent and were unique in the American literary world. Later, he devoted all his efforts to "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream," which was even more admired by the literary world, and his position as a playwright was stabilized and his name became prominent.

After he wrote "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream," he made a special trip to California. During his pilgrimage to Hollywood, he personally visited James Whale, the director of Universal Pictures in Universal City, and discussed with him how to bring "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream" to the screen. Whale, who knew the value of the work, naturally welcomed him very much. With the approval of Carl Laemmle Jr., the head of Universal Pictures, the filming was scheduled to begin under the direction of Whale. Usually, screenwriters in Hollywood did not have much close contact with film companies. The script was submitted, the fee was paid, and the literary transaction was completed. As for how the script was divided into scenes and how it was filmed, there were people responsible for handling it, and the author never asked. However, Sherwood was different. He broke the old routine with a punch, took the fee but did not leave, always hiding in the studio, following Whale to see how his "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream" was being adapted into a film.

Whale is not a casual director. At least, his ideas and talent are above Ernst Lubitsch, although he is far inferior to Charlie Chaplin. Therefore, Sherwood was inexplicably amazed after seeing a few scenes directed by him. He then affirmed that no one could direct his "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream" except Whale. He then bid farewell to Whale, left Universal City, and returned to his residence. When he left Universal City, he made a few remarks:

"I know that no one is qualified to direct "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream" as much as Whale because he completely organized London after the fierce bombing by the Air Force in 1917. That is the most important point of imagery in the whole play, which I deliberately expressed in the script. "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream" is not organized by a typical story. It is a reflection of the emotions of the general public who were severely oppressed during the war. The focus of the whole play is on that very organization.

"As a result of visiting "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream" in the studio, I proved that several very important parts really made me admit that Ms. Moe Clarke performed very brilliantly, vividly as if the real Myra (the character in the play) in my script ran out. That American singer who lives in London, she is completely affected by the war and feels endless hardships and difficulties in life, and at the same time suffers all kinds of traumas in the process of love. Ms. Mae's extraordinary performance is something I have never seen before. Therefore, Myra's pain as a singer who became one of the wailing people during the war was vividly conveyed between Ms. Mae's expressions to arouse the audience's emotion. Ms. Mae was specially hired to play the difficult part of Myra. It is not easy to perform the role of Myra in "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream." Only Ms. Mae can perform it. I am really impressed by her performance skills. Several shots of her co-starring with male actor Kent Douglass are also very brilliant.

The film adaptation of "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream" is so extraordinary that it makes me infinitely happy and satisfied because I like this script more deeply than anything I have written before."

After Sherwood gave his speech, he fell silent, but he was still meditating and pursuing his subject, probably looking for his next script.

(III) Director James Whale

Among the staff of a film production, the director is second only to the author in importance. If the director has talent, knowledge, and can see through the mysteries of the original meaning of a script, the release of the film will naturally have many amazing aspects. If he is a mediocre person, then even if the script is written very brilliantly, it will be ruined by that mediocre person. But this is not what I am talking about James Whale. James Whale's name has soared to the sky because of the successful direction of "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream." However, this director, who has the skill to elaborate on the essence of the script, did not develop his talent in one day. He was originally a playwright, born in Great Britain on July 2, 1896, but he was quiet and taciturn from youth to old age. He studied in England but never received a university education. He had served in the military and been an officer. During the European War, he was captured by the Germans and became a prisoner of war. He spent two years in a German prison.

In prison, he became aware of drama, noticed the expression of theatrical scenes, and began his drama work in prison until the end of the war. When the armistice was signed, he returned to England and staged the American historical drama "Lincoln" in England. Then he went to London to realize his drama life. In the course of his progress and success, his works were very amazing and produced in large quantities. The most successful ones include "The Cherry Orchard," "Prisoners of War," "The Seagull," and others.

Since Whale had achieved success in acting, he took a further step to devote himself to directing. Directing is more difficult than acting because both sides need to have a deep understanding of personality. There are also various other controls, deliberations, and arrangements. But Whale, during the trial period, with his rich knowledge, also gained considerable results and gradually made progress, standing in an important position in the British drama scene. The play "Journey's End" was his greatest success in directing.

The success of "Journey's End" made him expand his ambition and increase his desire. Perhaps he was tired of playing in drama and wanted to enter the field of film and become an old gardener. Film is even more different than drama. Although some people say that the basic principles of film and drama are the same, at least space and time are much wider than drama. In terms of organization, they are also completely different. However, Whale, who is both talented and knowledgeable, just fits the old saying "The capable can do anything." He actually achieved success. Based on his inherent knowledge and talent, he filmed his "Journey's End" and also came to Hollywood in the United States, occupying a chair in the director's seat of Universal Pictures in Universal City. Now, he has shouldered a heavy burden and successfully created Sherwood's masterpiece "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream." "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream" is not easy to direct. It is a difficult task in the film industry, but Whale took it up resolutely and achieved success, which is truly amazing.

This talented director is a tall, silent Englishman with a calm mind and a peaceful attitude. He always observes things first and then implements them. He has self-confidence but is unwilling to be reckless. This kind of dignified and steady ability to handle affairs can make people imagine his talent. Therefore, the success of Sherwood's "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream" is due to his calm mind, keen eyes, calm spirit, and broad knowledge.

(IV) Starring Mae Clarke

After introducing the two giants, the third one to be introduced is the star Mae Clarke. Like Whale, Ms. Mae did not graduate from college, but with her family's background, she is very authentic as a film actor. She is just over twenty years old, and her oval face has a unique beauty. She has a unique style outside of Greta Garbo, Marlene Dietrich, Joan Crawford, and Clara Bow. She is a blonde beauty with a pool of autumn water in her eyes, lined with two moth eyebrows, which is most feminine. Her 110-pound, five-foot-high delicate body is lively and graceful, graceful and healthy, with smooth skin, and has all the beauty of all beauties, and her talent is even more clever, and her manners are even more endearing. Such a talented woman makes her performance even more amazing and natural, making people see her unusually rich talent for acting. She acts in movies like mercury, penetrating every pore. Her deep understanding of the characters is not something that other actresses with star titles can match. That is her greatness, which is a shocking technique that has been gained through years of research and integrated with her talent. She has acted in quite a few films, but the blind directors have not understood her beauty and talent, so she has always been inferior to others. There is no Bole in the world, but there are many good horses. I cannot bear to mourn for Mae Clarke's lack of talent. However, such a talented and beautiful film actor will eventually reveal her brilliance and will not be submerged for a long time.

Sure enough, she was specially selected by Whale, who has unique insight, from among all the beauties to play the heroine of "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream." Only heroes can recognize heroes, as Whale is.

Mae's performance is purely based on the heart of the character, using her excellent talent to perform a certain emotion of the character. In "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream," we see on the scene that it is not Mae Clarke but Myra. Only those with deep cultivation can have great talent. Mae, who was not recognized in the past, is the reason why she has deep cultivation. Otherwise, relying solely on talent would not have today's achievements. After she became the heroine of "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream," her unprecedented performance was praised by all parties. The young head of Universal signed a five-year long-term contract with her to be the basic star of his company in order to realize his strong film development plan.

(V) Explanation of the Title

Regarding the title of Waterloo Bridge of "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream," everyone regards it as strange. Indeed, the title of a film is often taken from an unusual and novel name. Just like adopting an unusual and novel story as the story in the play, this proves that Sherwood is very familiar with London. The reason why his script takes the bridge as the background of the whole play is that the focus of each stage of the bridge cannot be separated, and the focus of each stage of the bridge cannot be separated from a beautiful word, and the beautiful part is especially at the end of the West, which is the fade-out in the film from both sides to the south bank of the river.

According to Londoners themselves, 19 people say that Waterloo Bridge is the most beautiful place and the main road for transportation between London and the world. Historically, it is also the most glorious and beautiful bridge on the entire Thames River. Italian sculptor Canova also praised it infinitely and said that it is most valuable to go from Rome to see this solemn and magnificent model of architecture.

The construction of Waterloo Bridge began in October 1811 and was completed on July 18, 1817. The engineer in charge was J.R. Rennie, a famous architect with rich knowledge and experience who had built several magnificent bridges. When building Waterloo Bridge, he was responsible for all the planning. The bridge was originally planned to be 1,326 feet long, but it was expanded to 2,456 feet long and 142 feet wide due to special decorations. The regular road is 70 feet wide and 654 feet high. The construction cost was £1 million. It was originally named "Bin Bridge" because it is an important bridge connecting Wellington Street and the riverside from the south. But in 1816, the year before its completion, it was named Waterloo Bridge. The Battle of Waterloo in the Anglo-French War on June 18, 1815, was a particularly glorious victory for the British army. In order to commemorate that battle, it was named Waterloo Bridge, and the Crown Prince personally officiated at the opening ceremony.

The focus of the film's story is borrowed from the glorious Waterloo Bridge in history as the background. The author took the name of the bridge as the title of the film. Therefore, the Waterloo Bridge is not only passed down in history, but now it is famous in film, and its popularity is even more indescribable.

(VI) Sketch

The reason why this film is wonderful, I think, is that the narrative of the facts is both charming and sad, the description of the plot is also bizarre and beautiful, and the performance of the scene is even more wonderful. Film, I often say, whether its theme is about the love of children or a glimpse of life, there is always a central consciousness, that is, the heresy of art. For example, "Broken Bridge, Lingering Dream," although the background is Waterloo Bridge in the war era, and the story is about the depression of London society during the war, its mission is to guide the people to arm themselves and go to the front line in accordance with our Chinese saying, "The rise and fall of the world is the responsibility of every individual." Because going to the front line, the situation in London gradually became bleak, and because Waterloo Bridge was attacked by the German Air Force, this sad and beautiful story was created. The foreign Qiu Jiu are all "loving the country without forgetting love." Therefore, the male character in the film is such a young man. After retreating from the front line, he met the infinitely sad and beautiful girl on Waterloo Bridge. The girl is a thin-fate person who has fallen to the end of the world. From the United States to London, she made a living by selling songs on the stage. She has turned over many romantic officers, and young masters, but because of the desolation of London, she eventually became a fallen flower. She was doing the business of the Wushan goddess on Waterloo Bridge. When she saw the young soldier, she suddenly tied him with her heart. However, in the era of turmoil, good young people are going to sacrifice for the country, and there are also grades. The girl then endured the pain and gave up her love, declined the young man's tenderness, and cut off her love to make him give up the idea and go to the front line to kill the enemy again.

However, the young man, who is deeply passionate, must be brave in his actions. Therefore, before returning to the front line after his leave, he ran to Waterloo Bridge to find the girl again. He found the girl, shamed him, insulted him, and beat him, but he was always as gentle as before, understanding everything, and it was necessary for the girl to allow him to go to the front line to sacrifice for the country. Passionate women sometimes have to abandon their private feelings and encourage the men they love with great righteousness. The girl then allowed him and wanted him to go to the front line. Unexpectedly, a farewell became a farewell forever. When waving a towel to say goodbye on Waterloo Bridge, she and a corner of Waterloo Bridge became powder together.

Oh, young men and women of China, I hope that you will look at this film and have some understanding of its focus.

Commercial News 194

Guoguang Manufacturing Company announced that the merchant Zhang Zhenting was extremely indignant at the violent sun invading China. He specially gathered friends to organize and establish the Guoguang Manufacturing Company, advocating domestic products, recovering rights and interests, and implementing the plan of saving the country through industry. They are now working hard to manufacture several kinds of towel racks, clothes racks, soap racks, and powder box racks. Preparations are complete and they will be launched soon. They will soon publish an advertisement to hire 20 salesmen, etc.

Dahua Glasses Company, located at the north end of Yokohama Bridge on North Sichuan Road, announced that from today onwards, all customers who purchase or repair glasses at the retail department will receive a set of exquisite calendars. This calendar is drawn and inscribed by the famous artist Wan Laiming, and is exquisitely printed in five colors, which is extremely beautiful, etc.

Medical News 195

Shen Jicang, an expert in internal medicine, has set up a clinic on Route Père Huc (now Route Sud) in the French Concession. His medical skills are profound and he has both learning and experience, which has gained the belief of patients. He also benefits the poor. He does not charge for visits to the poor, which is praised by the public. Recently, he was hired by the Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts as a school doctor, so his clinic is even busier, etc.
